5a3(20): nga zhi tshom ma skyes nang/ ma rig 'khrul so sol a yinng/ rig pa skod pa'i rnying so can// rnying po dge yais zin pa'i tsheng/ tshol sgrub 'ghrals sol ba yin / rgyud kyi / 
5a4(20): bya ba thong pa'i shing/ zhin chag 'khrul sa sol ba yin/ gnyin so grong du gyur pa'i tshing/ rkyen gyi 'khrual sa sol ba yin / ypo bes grong du gyung pa'i tsheg/ ma rtogs /

5b4(20): la bga yinng/ bya bral 'dzin sa co sa ni// ma bsn po ma'i la ba yin/ 'ghrul pas mi brdibs ypobs ning/ rog s tshung gi lu ba yin / ma hri ma bskol mi / 
5b5(20): gnas na// yin min min pa'i la ba yin / spros pa'i chos rnams thug grol nas / phyor bral chen po'i la ba yin/ rkyen rtog kha r+yu mi tog nang/ lta ba go ng du 
5b6(20): rkyol ba yin/ bongo 'ob khyad par la mzong na/ thig l nyag gcig la ba yin/ bzang ngan blang nre laM kyi na/ 'khral s+dzog mid gus sa yin/ mnyam byi hes sa min/ 
6a1(20): / kyi na// blo yis nhes s chos las grol ba yin// sems la 'khru 'kghrig mi za na// go rtog nang nas thung ba ying/ 
6a2(20): snang na yul ghyis mi gno na// phyi yi sgro 'o g tshos ying/ ben pa'iona yi chos na / nang gi rgyo 'o a tshod pa yin / sdug bsngal shes pa mi 'byung nang/ lda ba gnan la hisg/ 
6a3(20): sa yin / d/ g shig shes sa mi skye nang/ tid chen gnad kyis zin pa yin/ 'gyud lhog shes sa mi skyes nang/ rig sa gnang la phes pa yin/ 'khrul pa'i shesngs mi rkye na // 
6a4(20): go ng gi bna la phebs pa yin/ rgyu rkyen chos la csha rkyi nan/ rang byung gann la phebs pa yin / rig sa 'chal thas s+dzogs s nang/ skobs kyi gna la tshebs pa yin/ snong pa phyal / 
6a5(20): bsra ma song nas/ rig pa gnan la tshebs pa yin/ rig sa gzung 'dzin mi rkye nang/ sdong pa gnang la phis sa yin/ rig song tha d mi skye nang/ gnyis me gna la pheb pa yin //

6b1(20): 'on skad o sol ba'i chos dzes la/ sems sa' rdo rjyes yang mo sos sa/ la ba ldog nas bsgoms pa'i onng/ rnyisu byurg du yongam medg// skadg gosol pa'i khig gson nas / 
6b2(20): gsang ba a chen seMs lan btab pa// la bsgoms brkol ba med pa la / lha bzhin gnas pa bsgom pa yin/ bsgom btzhig 'chang bang lta ba yin/ lha rdob khyen ba'i rkyon las /

7a1(20): gnas pa'i mchag// de 'dzin nyams sa blung ba'i chos// nyid thams kgyaM smra// ng 'dzin 'byung 'jug l par gnas=log rgyun 'ga's/

7b6(20): gol sgrib r+yad ba bcad/ 'phrang gsum nang du bsku pa btsung la / s+dzong gsam nang du gcsig la ba' / rgyal po btson du bzung ba dang / bron s kyar la gdon pa dang/ gra'i /

8a3(20): lig rzes lang/ so 'i he la sogs pag/ gsang ba ga chon po'i rang bzhin gyis/ so la bgrib brnyar ba tshong sa'i / nyams brang myed pa 'di gsongs/ rig pa'i rnying s nyams /

8a5(20): bag char grib ha sring/ rang byung yo shes nyams brangs na / rgyu rkyen cos la sgro b rkyi// lus ngag yi gsal ci spyad kyang / ge chen spor la 'grung ldog lo' // srdogs nyis/

8b1(20): kyi spyod pa zas// / man pa'i sems la bsdan pa yin// go po'i yi chos ma brkyed spang/ na ba'i mig la blo god sa / kun tu bzang por khas blangs kyang / sola pa 'brul /
